* # **SPACEPORT**

* #### **A 'spaceport' is a site capable of launching spacecraft into interplanetary trajectories, the same way a *seaport* is for launching boats, and an *airport* is for launching aircraft.**

* #### **This 'spaceport' is for launching *YOU\!***

* #### **Think of it as a 'Youport'... a platform for launching *you* into your next steps along your (r)evolutionary [Path](http://path.mystrikingly.com).**

* #### **We hope you do what matters most, and have as much Fun as [you](http://parts.mystrikingly.com) can\!**

* #### **As consciousness-explorer Joseph Chilton Pearce says, *“Perhaps the scope of this work sounds a bit broad for a single volume, and I can hear complaints that I attempt too much. But I argue that all too often we attempt too little. Better an impossible task of splendid proportion than a sure but piddling one of no consequence. We learn from failures as well as successes.”***

* #### **As Lee Lozowick would say, *“If it is not impossible, why bother doing it?”***

* ### **NOTE: This is a directory of interlinked websites in the free-to-play massively-multiplayer online-and-offline thoughtware-upgrade matrix-building personal-transformation real-life adventure-game called [StartOver.xyz](http://startoverxyz.mystrikingly.com). Each website is a [doorway](http://spaceport.mystrikingly.com/) to [context](http://setcontext.mystrikingly.com) and [experiments](http://becomeanexperimenter.mystrikingly.com) that [upgrade your thoughtware](http://boxtechnology.mystrikingly.com) so you can relocate your [point of origin](http://pointoforigin.mystrikingly.com/) to 'next culture' \- [Archiarchy](http://archiarchy.mystrikingly.com) \- and can [create](http://creation.mystrikingly.com) more [clarity](http://swordofclarity.mystrikingly.com) and [possibility](http://mapofpossibility.mystrikingly.com/) [for delivering the](https://spaceport.mystrikingly.com/) nonmaterial value [of your](https://spaceport.mystrikingly.com/) Archetypal Lineage . Your [knowledge](http://experientialreality.mystrikingly.com/) is what you think *about*. Your [thoughtware](http://thoughtware.mystrikingly.com) is what you use to think *with*. When you [change your thoughtware](http://phase1phase2.mystrikingly.com), you go through a [liquid state](http://liquidstate.mystrikingly.com) as your mind [reorganizes](http://phoenixprocess.mystrikingly.com) itself. Liquid states can bring up transformational [feelings](http://4feelings.mystrikingly.com) and [emotions](http://4emotions.mystrikingly.com). By [upgrading your thoughtware](http://alifeoflearning.mystrikingly.com) you [build matrix](http://buildmatrix.mystrikingly.com) to hold more [consciousness](http://wholepermaculture.mystrikingly.com/) and leave behind a [Low Drama](http://lowdrama.mystrikingly.com/) life of [reactivity](http://reactivity.mystrikingly.com/). No one can upgrade your thoughtware for you. More interestingly, no one can stop you from upgrading your thoughtware. Our theory is that when we [collectively build](http://alifeofpractice.mystrikingly.com) 1,000,000 new Matrix Points we will change the morphogenetic field of the human race for the better. Please choose [responsibly](http://radicalresponsibility.mystrikingly.com) to read these websites. Reading this whole website is worth 1 Matrix Point. Doing any of the experiments earns you additional Matrix Points. Please use Matrix Code SPACEPOR.00 to log your Matrix Point for reading this website on [StartOver.xyz](http://startoverxyz.mystrikingly.com/). Thank you for playing full out\!**

* ### **Archan Law**

* ###### [**archanlaw.mystrikingly.com**](http://archanlaw.mystrikingly.com)

* The Rule Of Law of modern culture is [exterminating life on Earth](http://whatnow.mystrikingly.com) at the fastest possible rate. Anyone following the Rule Of Law of modern culture is criminally insane. Anyone enforcing the Rule Of Law of modern culture has already [forfeited their life](http://psychopath.mystrikingly.com).  
* [Archiarchy](http://archiarchy.mystrikingly.com) implements an entirely different Rule Of Law, the Law of  [Radical Responsibility](http://radicalresponsibility.mystrikingly.com) centered on [Authentic](http://becomeauthentic.mystrikingly.com) [Adulthood](http://adulthood.mystrikingly.com) [Initiatory](http://initiations.mystrikingly.com) [Processess](http://process.mystrikingly.com). Anything not [Regenerative](http://regenerative.mystrikingly.com) is illegal in Archiarchy, which adopts a Bill Of Wrongs rather than a Bill Of Rights. Archiarchy implements Universal Jurisdiction and Citizen Arrests, [Emotional Healing Processes](http://emotionalhealingprocess.mystrikingly.com), [Torus Meeting Technology](http://torustechnology.mystrikingly.com), etc.  
* Archan Law is a [Specialty in Possibilitator Training](https://possibilitatortraining.mystrikingly.com/#specialties).  
* It is time.  
* There is a new future.  
* *This is the way.*  
* Also see:  
* [gameworldtheory.mystrikingly.com](http://gameworldtheory.mystrikingly.com)  
* [regenerateearthgoals.mystrikingly.com](http://regenerateearthgoals.mystrikingly.com)

* ###### [**archiarchy.mystrikingly.com**](http://archiarchy.mystrikingly.com)

* Archiarchy is the regenerative local-authority initiation-centered culture that is naturally emerging around the world now that matriarchy and patriarchy have run their course.  
* Also see:  
* [patriarchy.mystrikingly.com](http://patriarchy.mystrikingly.com)

* ### **Experience Archiarchy \- a travelguide**

* ###### [**experiencearchiarchy.mystrikingly.com**](https://experiencearchiarchy.mystrikingly.com)

* There are guide books for countries and cities, but none yet for Archiarchy. This is the first. There will also be an *Archiarchy Phrase Book* to help you learn the language\!  
  Some [Archans](https://archan.mystrikingly.com) who are currently nomadic, will be visiting Archan-type projects and researching possible entries for the guide book. Let us know if you are one\!

* ### **Magic Cow Bridgehouse** 

* ### **(New York)**

* ###### [**magiccowbridgehouse.wordpress.com**](http://magiccowbridgehouse.wordpress.com)

* We know it is out there: it is possible for people to live together in a more loving, connected, and empowered way. A way where our Beings align with archetypal forces and create spaces for things like Love or Transformation. But how do we get there? How do we transform the parts of ourselves that block this kind of living and create separateness or smallness? The way we’ve found is to live in [Radical Responsibility](http://radicalresponsibility.mystrikingly.com). Magic Cow Bridgehouse is in New York.

* ### **Deconstellation**

* ###### [**deconstellation.mystrikingly.com**](http://deconstellation.mystrikingly.com)

* (one of the [PM Adulthood Initiation Processes](http://pmprocesses.mystrikingly.com))  
* Many people adopted the [Survival Strategy](http://survivalstrategy.mystrikingly.com) of mapping on to the Survival Strategy of one of their parents or grandparents. This role model fills up their interior with 'not themselves'. We have discovered that it is possible in a Possibility Coaching EHP to Deconstellate you from your Family Constellation by giving an artifact of the role model back to the person you copied it from.  
* broken image

* ### **Deconstructions**

* ###### [**deconstructions.mystrikingly.com**](http://deconstructions.mystrikingly.com)

* (one of the [PM Adulthood Initiation Processes](http://pmprocesses.mystrikingly.com))  
* Many people adopt the [Survival Strategy](http://survivalstrategy.mystrikingly.com) of building a [Memetic Construct](http://memeticconstruct.mystrikingly.com) inside of themselves as a [belief](http://beliefs.mystrikingly.com) system or [world view](http://boxtechnology.mystrikingly.com), a [story](http://storyworld.mystrikingly.com) that they regard as immutable. This [Inner Structure](http://innerstructure.mystrikingly.com) then serves as an abode for random 'Riders', energetic vampire entities that feed on your energy and can prevent physical and psycho-emotional imbalances from healing. We have discovered that through a Possibility Coaching Deconstruction Process you can Deconstruct your Memetic Construct, thus removing the home of the parasites who are then easy to flush out, thus allowing the needed healing to occur.  
* broken image

* ### **Decontamination**

* ###### [**decontamination.mystrikingly.com**](http://decontamination.mystrikingly.com)

* Our Research Teams have discovered the long hard slow way that many more people than we ever imagined adopted the [Survival Strategy](http://survivalstrategy.mystrikingly.com) of Contaminating their [Adult Egostate](http://egostate.mystrikingly.com) with their Child, Parent, Gremlin, or Demon Egostate. This blocks them from [Connection](http://fearofconnection.mystrikingly.com), [Healing](http://3phasehealing.mystrikingly.com)[,](https://spaceport.mystrikingly.com/) and [Authentic Adulthood Initiations](http://initiations.mystrikingly.com). Decontaminating the Child Egostate, Parent Egostate, Gremlin Egostate, and Demon Egostate out of the [Adult Egostate](http://egostate.mystrikingly.com) depends on first succeeding with [Gremlin Transformation](http://gremlintransformation.mystrikingly.com) and recovering from [Dramaholism](https://dramaholic.mystrikingly.com). Successfully accomplishing [Gremlin Transformation](http://gremlintransformation.mystrikingly.com) is a prerequisite for beginning Decontaminations.  
* (a [3 Phase Healing](http://3phasehealing.mystrikingly.com) process, and one of the [PM Processes](http://pmprocesses.mystrikingly.com))  
* Also see:  
* [gremlintransformation.mystrikingly.com](https://gremlintransformation.mystrikingly.com)  
* [dramaholic.mystrikingly.com](https://dramaholic.mystrikingly.com)  
* [baggage.mystrikingly.com](http://baggage.mystrikingly.com)  
* [addicted.mystrikingly.com](https://addicted.mystrikingly.com)  
* [gremlinselfcannibalism.mystrikingly.com](https://gremlinselfcannibalism.mystrikingly.com)  
* [gremlinviolence.mystrikingly.com](https://gremlinviolence.mystrikingly.com)  
* [egostate.mystrikingly.com](https://egostate.mystrikingly.com)  
* broken image

* ### **Possibility Management \- Home**

* ###### [**possibilitymanagement.org**](https://possibilitymanagement.org)

* This is the home base for the Possibility Management gameworld. It tells you what [Possibility Management](https://possibilitymanagement.org/about/) is, how to learn it in trainings such as [*Expand The Box*](https://possibilitymanagement.org/doingit/etb/) and [*Possibility Labs*](https://possibilitymanagement.org/doingit/plabs/), how to practice it in [Possibility Teams](https://possibilitymanagement.org/doingit/#courses) and [Possibility Coaching](https://possibilitymanagement.org/doingit/coaching/), and how to learn to [serve as a Possibility Management Trainer](https://possibilitymanagement.org/doingit/tslabs/). It also provides a [calendar of events](https://possibilitymanagement.org/calendar/) and a [list of Possibility Management trainers](https://possibilitymanagement.org/trainers/).  
* broken image

* ### **Quit School**

* Yes, you can Quit School.  
* Even if you are 50 years old, you can get out of the conforming, adaptive, self-disempowering survival habits that you adopted while you were a student in school.  
* Do you think it is about time?

* ### **Radical Freedom**

* ###### [**radicalfreedom.mystrikingly.com**](http://radicalfreedom.mystrikingly.com)

* If you manipulate yourself to do what you already want to do, then you are afraid of someone else enough to give them power over your life. In other words, you are not free to begin your Adulthood journey. Is it time to leave adolescence behind but not time to start your initiations? Then it is time for a year or two of Radical Freedom. What are you waiting for?  
* Also see:  
* [adulthood.mystrikingly.com](http://adulthood.mystrikingly.com)

* ### **Regenerate Earth Goals (REGs)**

* ###### [**regenerateearthgoals.mystrikingly.com**](http://regenerateearthgoals.mystrikingly.com)

* The popularized United Nations' SDGs (Sustainable Development Goals) are no longer valid. Nothing about modern culture can be 'sustained' without further exterminating life on Earth. Possibility Management formally proposes (December 2023\) to replace SDGs with REGs (Regenerate Earth Goals), as part of the September 2024 United Nations [Summit Of The Future](https://www.un.org/en/summit-of-the-future) to create a new Pact For The Future.  
* Also see:  
* [whatnow.mystrikingly.com](http://whatnow.mystrikingly.com)

* [un.org/en/summit-of-the-future](https://www.un.org/en/summit-of-the-future)

* ### **robert wolff**

* ### **author of the inspiring and highly recommended book: [*Original Wisdom*](https://bookshop.org/a/16582/9780892818662)**

* ### **MATRIX CODE: BOOK0142.00**

* ###### [**wildwolff.mystrikingly.com**](http://wildwolff.mystrikingly.com)

* When researcher and author robert wolff died in 2015 there was no one who took over maintaining his generous website where he offered all his writings and musings, always downloadable for free. The realization that all robert's gifts might suddenly vanish from the world was a shock to me, so I stepped up and built up a replacement website using the same URL he chose: wildwolff. If you have saved something of his that you think should go there, please send it to me and I will upload it. Thank you\! Meanwhile, happy reading\!  
* \- Clinton Callahan  
* Also see:  
* [possibilitybooks.mystrikingly.com](http://possibilitybooks.mystrikingly.com)  
* Roll The Energy, StartOver.xyz, Possibility Management

* ### **SPARK Experiments (English)**

* ### ***"Every revolution begins with a spark..."***

* ###### [**sparks-english.mystrikingly.com**](http://sparks-english.mystrikingly.com)

* S.P.A.R.K. stands for 'Specific Practical Applications of Radical Knowledge'. Reading a S.P.A.R.K. earns you 1 Matrix Point in the [StartOver.xyz](https://howtoplay.mystrikingly.com) game. Doing any of the S.P.A.R.K. Experiments earns you additional Matrix Points. Doing S.P.A.R.K. Experiments upgrades your [thoughtware](http://thoughtware.mystrikingly.com) [because S.P.A.R.K.s are](https://spaceport.mystrikingly.com/) [written memetically](http://memetics.mystrikingly.com). Upgrading your thoughtware changes the morphogenetic field of the human race, which may be the most powerful force (outside of global warming...) for changing the status quo. S.P.A.R.K.s are [thoughtware for Archiarchy](http://50thoughtwareupgrades.mystrikingly.com).  
* S.P.A.R.K.s are available in a growing number of languages.  
* [You can help](http://pmtranslators.mystrikingly.com).  
* Also see:  
* [possibilitatorresources.mystrikingly.com](http://possibilitatorresources.mystrikingly.com)  
* [distinctionary.mystrikingly.com](http://distinctionary.mystrikingly.com)

* ### **Zombies**

* ###### [**zombies.mystrikingly.com**](http://zombies.mystrikingly.com)

* You support the [Values](https://values.mystrikingly.com) of any [Gameworld](https://gameworldtheory.mystrikingly.com) in which you participate.  
* We define a 'Zombie' as 'anyone who is not aware of the Values of the Gameworlds in which they participate'.  
* [SPARK232](http://sparks.nextculture.org/res/sparks/Spark-232-en.pdf) says: *Thinking there is a plan for what to do next makes you a Zombie.*  
* Also see:  
* [whatnow.mystrikingly.com](http://whatnow.mystrikingly.com)  
* [values.mystrikingly.com](http://values.mystrikingly.com)  
* [guardianship.mystrikingly.com](https://guardianship.mystrikingly.com)  
* [youandyourjob.mystrikingly.com](http://youandyourjob.mystrikingly.com)  
* [thehierarchy.mystrikingly.com](http://thehierarchy.mystrikingly.com)  
* [patriarchy.mystrikingly.com](http://patriarchy.mystrikingly.com)  
* [psychopath.mystrikingly.com](http://psychopath.mystrikingly.com)  
* [swordofclarity.mystrikingly.com](http://swordofclarity.mystrikingly.com)  
* [setcontext.mystrikingly.com](http://setcontext.mystrikingly.com)  
* [culturetoculture.mystrikingly.com](http://culturetoculture.mystrikingly.com)  
* [healfromschool.mystrikingly.com](http://healfromschool.mystrikingly.com)  
* [authority.mystrikingly.com](http://authority.mystrikingly.com) Zombieism is cured through a person taking back [radical](http://radicalresponsibility.mystrikingly.com) personal Authority.  
* "*Every person we save is one less Zombie we have to fight*." (...from the film [*World War Z*](https://www.imdb.com/title/tt0816711/).)

* ### **DIRECTORY OF POSSIBILITY MANAGEMENT (PM) WEBSITES**

  * To search the StartOver.xyz univere, please use: [nextculturenow.com/possibility-search](https://nextculturenow.com/possibility-search/)  
  * To arrange a free 30 minute 'hello PM' call for no reason, please visit: [discoverycall.mystrikingly.com](http://discoverycall.mystrikingly.com)  
  * To find your way around the Possibility Management and Archiarchy universes, please visit: [foreverything.mystrikingly.com](http://foreverything.mystrikingly.com)  
  * To find links to Possibility Management resources, please visit our Linktree: [linktr.ee/possibilitymanagement](https://linktr.ee/possibilitymanagement)  
  * To learn HOW TO PLAY StartOver.xyz, please visit: [howtoplay.mystrikingly.com](http://howtoplay.mystrikingly.com)  
  * To explore the main StartOver.xyz website, please visit: startoverxyz.mystrikingly.com  
  * To register your [StartOverxyz.mystrikingly.com](http://startoverxyz.mystrikingly.com/) Matrix Points in your free account, please visit: [https://login.startover.xyz](https://login.startover.xyz/)  
  * To register for *Expand The Box* Training or Possibility Labs, please visit: [possibilitymanagement.org](http://possibilitymanagement.org/)

* ### [**StartOver.xyz**](http://howtoplay.mystrikingly.com)

* **NOTE:** This website is a [Bubble in the Bubble Map](http://howtoplay.mystrikingly.com/) of the free-to-playmassively-multiplayer online-and-offline thoughtware-upgrade matrix-building personal-transformation real-life adventure-game called [StartOver.xyz](http://startoverxyz.mystrikingly.com/). It is a [doorway](http://spaceport.mystrikingly.com/) to [experiments](http://becomeanexperimenter.mystrikingly.com/) that [upgrade your thoughtware](http://boxtechnology.mystrikingly.com/) so you can relocate your [point of origin](http://pointoforigin.mystrikingly.com/) and [create](http://creation.mystrikingly.com/) more [possibility](https://possibilitymanagement.org/). Your [knowledge](http://experientialreality.mystrikingly.com/) is what you think about. Your [thoughtware](http://thoughtware.mystrikingly.com/) is what you use to think with. When you [change your thoughtware](http://phase1phase2.mystrikingly.com/), you go through a [liquid state](http://liquidstate.mystrikingly.com/) as your mind [reorganizes](http://phoenixprocess.mystrikingly.com/) itself. Liquid states can bring up transformational [feelings](http://4feelings.mystrikingly.com/) and [emotions](http://4emotions.mystrikingly.com/). By [upgrading your thoughtware](http://alifeoflearning.mystrikingly.com/) you [build matrix](http://buildmatrix.mystrikingly.com/) to hold more [consciousness](http://wholepermaculture.mystrikingly.com/) and leave behind a [low drama](http://lowdrama.mystrikingly.com/) life of [reactivity](http://reactivity.mystrikingly.com/). No one can upgrade your thoughtware for you. More interestingly, no one can stop you from upgrading your thoughtware. Our theory is that when we [collectively build](http://alifeofpractice.mystrikingly.com/) 1,000,000 new Matrix Points we will change themorphogenetic field of the human race for the better. Please choose [responsibly](http://radicalresponsibility.mystrikingly.com/) to read this website. Reading this whole website is worth 1 Matrix Point. Doing any of the experiments earns you additional Matrix Points. Please use Matrix Code **SPACEPOR.00** to log your MatrixPoint for reading this website on [StartOver.xyz](http://startoverxyz.mystrikingly.com/). Thank you for playing full out\!
